<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><b>Item 3.01</b></span> <span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><b>Notice of Delisting or Failure to Satisfy a Continued Listing Rule or Standard; Transfer of Listing.</b></span></p>



<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">January
6, 2025, Alpha Modus Holdings, Inc. (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Company</span>&#8221;) received a written notice (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Notice</span>&#8221;) from
the Listing Qualifications Department of The Nasdaq Stock Market (&#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Nasdaq</span>&#8221;) indicating that the Company no longer
meets the minimum market value of publicly held shares (&#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">MVPHS</span>&#8221;) of $15,000,000 required by Nasdaq&#8217;s Listing
Rules (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Rules</span>&#8221;).</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">The
Notice has no immediate effect on the listing or trading of the Company&#8217;s securities, except that an indicator will be displayed
with quotation information related to the Company&#8217;s securities on NASDAQ.com and NASDAQTrader.com and may be displayed by other
third-party providers of market data information. If the Company fails to timely regain compliance with the Rules, the Company&#8217;s
securities will be subject to delisting from Nasdaq. Under the Rules, the Company has 180 calendar days, or until July 7, 2025, to
regain compliance. If the Company&#8217;s MVPHS closes at $15,000,000 or more for a minimum of ten consecutive business days during
this period, Nasdaq will provide the Company with written confirmation of compliance, and the matter will be closed.</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">If
the Company&#8217;s common stock ultimately were to be delisted for any reason, it could negatively impact the Company by (i) reducing
the liquidity and market price of the Company&#8217;s common stock; (ii) reducing the number of investors willing to hold or acquire
the Company&#8217;s common stock, which could negatively impact the Company&#8217;s ability to raise equity financing; (iii) limiting
the Company&#8217;s ability to use a registration statement to offer and sell freely tradable securities, thereby preventing the Company
from accessing the public capital markets; and (iv) impairing the Company&#8217;s ability to provide equity incentives to its employees.</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><b>Disclosure
Regarding Forward-Looking Information</b></span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">This
Current Report on Form 8-K contains forward-looking statements within the meaning of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of
1995. These forward-looking statements include, but are not limited to, statements regarding the Company&#8217;s beliefs and expectations
relating to the Company&#8217;s MVPHS, Nasdaq&#8217;s listing rules, and whether the Company&#8217;s common stock will remain listed
on Nasdaq. These forward-looking statements are based on the current beliefs and expectations of the Company&#8217;s management with
respect to future events, only speak as of the date that they are made and are subject to significant risks and uncertainties. Such statements
can be identified by the use of words such as &#8220;future,&#8221; &#8220;anticipates,&#8221; &#8220;believes,&#8221; &#8220;estimates,&#8221;
&#8220;expects,&#8221; &#8220;intends,&#8221; &#8220;plans,&#8221; &#8220;predicts,&#8221; &#8220;will,&#8221; &#8220;would,&#8221; &#8220;could,&#8221;
&#8220;continue,&#8221; &#8220;can,&#8221; &#8220;may,&#8221; &#8220;look forward,&#8221; &#8220;aim,&#8221; &#8220;hopes,&#8221; and
similar terms, although not all forward-looking statements contain such words or expressions. Actual results could differ significantly
from those set forth in the forward-looking statements.</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">Important
factors that may cause actual results to differ materially from those in the forward-looking statements include, but are not limited
to, a material delay in the Company&#8217;s financial reporting, the possibility that the Company is unable to regain compliance with,
or thereafter continue to comply with, Nasdaq&#8217;s listing rules, or experience violations of additional listing rules, the possibility
that Nasdaq may delist the Company&#8217;s securities and other factors contained in the &#8220;Risk Factors&#8221; section and elsewhere
in the Company&#8217;s filings with the SEC from time to time, including, but not limited to, its Annual Report on Form 10-K and its
Quarterly Reports on Form 10-Q. The Company does not undertake to update any forward-looking statements to reflect changed assumptions,
the impact of circumstances or events that may arise after the date of the forward-looking statements, or other changes over time, except
as required by law.</span></p>
